Shader "==PGAME==/LobbyPokemon/Extra/m_lob_ghostGlass_lv3" {
Properties {
[Header(Tex)] [MainTexture] _MainTex ("Diffiuse(RGB)厚度(A)", 2D) = "black" { }
_BumpMap ("Normal Map", 2D) = "bump" { }
_RampMap ("高光贴图", 2D) = "black" { }
_GhostMap ("渐隐贴图", 2D) = "black" { }
[Header(Common)] _ShadowOffset ("玻璃边缘厚度", Range(-2, 2)) = 0
_ShadowPow ("玻璃边缘软硬", Range(0, 10)) = 2
_ShadowScale ("折射强弱", Range(0, 1)) = 1
[HDR] _SHTopColor ("薄玻璃颜色", Color) = (2.5,2.5,2.5,1)
[HDR] _SHBotColor ("厚玻璃颜色", Color) = (2.5,2.5,2.5,1)
[Header(OutLine)] [KeywordEnum(OFF, ON)] _VTEX ("是否使用贴图控制定点色", Float) = 0
[KeywordEnum(OFF, ON)] _VCOLOR2N ("是否使用顶点色勾边优化", Float) = 0

_Offset ("Z Offset(深度偏移)", Float) = -5
_lightDir ("lightDirtion(勾边光源方向)", Vector) = (9.48,3.68,0,0)

#ifdef VERTEX
#version 100

uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_WorldTransformParams;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
uniform 	mediump float _MainlightAttenuation;
uniform 	mediump float _AddlightAttenuation;
uniform 	mediump float _AddlightLerp;
uniform 	mediump float _RimlightAttenuation;
attribute highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
attribute highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump float u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat18;
float u_xlat19;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.xzw = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat0.xzw, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * vec3(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat1.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * u_xlat1.xxx;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_4 = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4 * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_5.z = u_xlat16_4 * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_5.xz);
    u_xlat16_4 = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4 = u_xlat16_4 * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4 = u_xlat16_4 * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_4 = clamp(u_xlat16_4, 0.0, 1.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4 * u_xlat16_4;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

mediump float u_xlat16_21;

void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat22);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat22) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.zxy) * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat22);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat22) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat10_4.xyz = texture2D(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat10_4.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_0.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyw = u_xlat16_0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_0.xyw;
    u_xlat16_21 = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_21) * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat3.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat3.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = abs(u_xlat16_0.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_0.x = min(u_xlat16_0.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_7.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_7.x);
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xx * u_xlat3.xy;
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy + _Time.xx;
    u_xlat10_1.xyz = texture2D(_GhostMap, u_xlat1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat16_0.x + (-_ShadowOffset);
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat22 * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat22 = clamp(u_xlat22, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_21 = (-u_xlat22) + 1.0;
    u_xlat10_2 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_21 = u_xlat16_21 + u_xlat10_2.w;
    u_xlat16_21 = clamp(u_xlat16_21, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat3.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_21) * vec2(_ShadowScale) + u_xlat16_7.xy;
    u_xlat10_3 = texture2D(_RampMap, u_xlat3.xy);
    u_xlat16_4 = u_xlat10_3 * _SHTopColor;
    u_xlat16_3 = u_xlat10_3 * _SHBotColor + (-u_xlat16_4);
    u_xlat16_3 = vec4(u_xlat16_21) * u_xlat16_3 + u_xlat16_4;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_21 * _SHBotColor.w + u_xlat16_3.w;
    u_xlat16_7.x = clamp(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = dot(vec2(vec2(_Cutoff, _Cutoff)), u_xlat16_7.xx);
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat16_7.x + (-u_xlat16_0.x);
    u_xlat22 = clamp(u_xlat22, 0.0, 1.0);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat22;
    u_xlat6.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_0.xyz + u_xlat10_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = (-u_xlat16_3.xyz) + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(vec3(_Cutoff, _Cutoff, _Cutoff)) * u_xlat16_0.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) + u_xlat10_1.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(_GhostChange) * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    return;
}

    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * vec3(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat1.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * u_xlat1.xxx;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_4 = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4 * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_5.z = u_xlat16_4 * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_5.xz);
    u_xlat16_4 = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4 = u_xlat16_4 * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4 = u_xlat16_4 * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4 = min(max(u_xlat16_4, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4 = clamp(u_xlat16_4, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4 * u_xlat16_4;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;

    u_xlat22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat22);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat22) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.zxy) * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat22);

#else

#else
    u_xlat16_7.x = clamp(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

    u_xlat22 = u_xlat16_7.x + (-u_xlat16_0.x);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat22 = min(max(u_xlat22, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat22 = clamp(u_xlat22, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat22;
    u_xlat6.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_0.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = (-u_xlat16_3.xyz) + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(vec3(_Cutoff, _Cutoff, _Cutoff)) * u_xlat16_0.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(_GhostChange) * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_21 = (-u_xlat22) + 1.0;
    u_xlat10_2 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_21 = u_xlat16_21 + u_xlat10_2.w;
    u_xlat16_21 = clamp(u_xlat16_21, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat3.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_21) * vec2(_ShadowScale) + u_xlat16_7.xy;
    u_xlat10_3 = texture2D(_RampMap, u_xlat3.xy);
    u_xlat16_4 = u_xlat10_3 * _SHTopColor;
    u_xlat16_3 = u_xlat10_3 * _SHBotColor + (-u_xlat16_4);
    u_xlat16_3 = vec4(u_xlat16_21) * u_xlat16_3 + u_xlat16_4;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_21 * _SHBotColor.w + u_xlat16_3.w;
    u_xlat16_7.x = clamp(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = dot(vec2(vec2(_Cutoff, _Cutoff)), u_xlat16_7.xx);
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat16_7.x + (-u_xlat16_0.x);
    u_xlat22 = clamp(u_xlat22, 0.0, 1.0);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat22;
    u_xlat6.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_0.xyz + u_xlat10_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = (-u_xlat16_3.xyz) + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(vec3(_Cutoff, _Cutoff, _Cutoff)) * u_xlat16_0.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) + u_xlat10_1.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(_GhostChange) * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    return;
}

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump float u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat18;
float u_xlat19;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.xzw = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat0.xzw, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * vec3(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;

    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;

    u_xlat16_5.z = u_xlat16_4 * _RimlightAttenuation;

    u_xlat16_4 = u_xlat16_4 * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4 = u_xlat16_4 * _AddlightAttenuation;

    u_xlat16_4 = min(max(u_xlat16_4, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4 = clamp(u_xlat16_4, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4 * u_xlat16_4;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;

void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat22);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat22) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.zxy) * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat22);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat22) * u_xlat3.xyz;

    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_21) * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat3.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat3.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = abs(u_xlat16_0.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_0.x = min(u_xlat16_0.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_7.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_7.x);
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xx * u_xlat3.xy;
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy + _Time.xx;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_GhostMap, u_xlat1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat16_0.x + (-_ShadowOffset);
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat22 * _ShadowPow;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat22 = min(max(u_xlat22, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat22 = clamp(u_xlat22, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

    u_xlat16_21 = u_xlat16_21 + u_xlat16_2.w;

    u_xlat16_21 = min(max(u_xlat16_21, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_21 = clamp(u_xlat16_21, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat3.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_21) * vec2(_ShadowScale) + u_xlat16_7.xy;
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(_RampMap, u_xlat3.xy);
    u_xlat16_4 = u_xlat16_3 * _SHTopColor;
    u_xlat16_3 = u_xlat16_3 * _SHBotColor + (-u_xlat16_4);
    u_xlat16_3 = vec4(u_xlat16_21) * u_xlat16_3 + u_xlat16_4;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_21 * _SHBotColor.w + u_xlat16_3.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_7.x = min(max(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_7.x = clamp(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat16_7.x = dot(vec2(vec2(_Cutoff, _Cutoff)), u_xlat16_7.xx);
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat16_7.x + (-u_xlat16_0.x);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat22 = min(max(u_xlat22, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat22 = clamp(u_xlat22, 0.0, 1.0);

    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat22;
    u_xlat6.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_0.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;

uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_WorldTransformParams;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
uniform 	mediump float _MainlightAttenuation;
uniform 	mediump float _AddlightAttenuation;
uniform 	mediump float _AddlightLerp;
uniform 	mediump float _RimlightAttenuation;
attribute highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
attribute highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
varying highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump float u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat18;
float u_xlat19;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.xzw = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat0.xzw, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * vec3(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat1.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * u_xlat1.xxx;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_4 = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4 * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_5.z = u_xlat16_4 * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_5.xz);
    u_xlat16_4 = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4 = u_xlat16_4 * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4 = u_xlat16_4 * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_4 = clamp(u_xlat16_4, 0.0, 1.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4 * u_xlat16_4;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

precision highp int;
uniform 	vec4 _MainLightPosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainLightColor;
uniform 	vec4 _Time;

uniform lowp sampler2D _MainTex;
uniform lowp sampler2D _RampMap;
uniform lowp sampler2D _GhostMap;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
#define SV_Target0 gl_FragData[0]
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
lowp vec3 u_xlat10_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
lowp vec4 u_xlat10_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
lowp vec4 u_xlat10_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
lowp vec3 u_xlat10_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_7;
mediump float u_xlat16_21;
float u_xlat22;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat22);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat22) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.zxy) * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat22);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat22) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat10_4.xyz = texture2D(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat10_4.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_0.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyw = u_xlat16_0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_0.xyw;
    u_xlat16_21 = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_21) * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat3.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat3.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = abs(u_xlat16_0.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_0.x = min(u_xlat16_0.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_7.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_7.x);
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xx * u_xlat3.xy;
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy + _Time.xx;
    u_xlat10_1.xyz = texture2D(_GhostMap, u_xlat1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat16_0.x + (-_ShadowOffset);
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat22 * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat22 = clamp(u_xlat22, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_21 = (-u_xlat22) + 1.0;
    u_xlat10_2 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_21 = u_xlat16_21 + u_xlat10_2.w;
    u_xlat16_21 = clamp(u_xlat16_21, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat3.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_21) * vec2(_ShadowScale) + u_xlat16_7.xy;
    u_xlat10_3 = texture2D(_RampMap, u_xlat3.xy);
    u_xlat16_4 = u_xlat10_3 * _SHTopColor;
    u_xlat16_3 = u_xlat10_3 * _SHBotColor + (-u_xlat16_4);
    u_xlat16_3 = vec4(u_xlat16_21) * u_xlat16_3 + u_xlat16_4;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_21 * _SHBotColor.w + u_xlat16_3.w;
    u_xlat16_7.x = clamp(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = dot(vec2(vec2(_Cutoff, _Cutoff)), u_xlat16_7.xx);
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat16_7.x + (-u_xlat16_0.x);
    u_xlat22 = clamp(u_xlat22, 0.0, 1.0);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat22;
    u_xlat6.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_0.xyz + u_xlat10_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = (-u_xlat16_3.xyz) + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(vec3(_Cutoff, _Cutoff, _Cutoff)) * u_xlat16_0.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) + u_xlat10_1.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(_GhostChange) * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _RampMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _GhostMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_7;
mediump float u_xlat16_21;
float u_xlat22;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat22);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat22) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.zxy) * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat22);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat22) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_0.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyw = u_xlat16_0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_0.xyw;
    u_xlat16_21 = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_21) * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat3.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat3.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = abs(u_xlat16_0.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_0.x = min(u_xlat16_0.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_7.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_7.x);
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xx * u_xlat3.xy;
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy + _Time.xx;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_GhostMap, u_xlat1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat16_0.x + (-_ShadowOffset);
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat22 * _ShadowPow;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat22 = min(max(u_xlat22, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat22 = clamp(u_xlat22, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_21 = (-u_xlat22) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_21 = u_xlat16_21 + u_xlat16_2.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_21 = min(max(u_xlat16_21, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_21 = clamp(u_xlat16_21, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat3.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_21) * vec2(_ShadowScale) + u_xlat16_7.xy;
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(_RampMap, u_xlat3.xy);
    u_xlat16_4 = u_xlat16_3 * _SHTopColor;
    u_xlat16_3 = u_xlat16_3 * _SHBotColor + (-u_xlat16_4);
    u_xlat16_3 = vec4(u_xlat16_21) * u_xlat16_3 + u_xlat16_4;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_21 * _SHBotColor.w + u_xlat16_3.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_7.x = min(max(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_7.x = clamp(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_7.x = dot(vec2(vec2(_Cutoff, _Cutoff)), u_xlat16_7.xx);
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat16_7.x + (-u_xlat16_0.x);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat22 = min(max(u_xlat22, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat22 = clamp(u_xlat22, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat22;
    u_xlat6.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_0.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = (-u_xlat16_3.xyz) + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(vec3(_Cutoff, _Cutoff, _Cutoff)) * u_xlat16_0.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(_GhostChange) * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    return;
}

"// hash: a44aa971ec49478
#ifdef VERTEX
#version 300 es

#define HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS 1
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
#define UNITY_UNIFORM
#else
#define UNITY_UNIFORM uniform
#endif
#define UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION 1
#if UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION
#define UNITY_LOCATION(x) layout(location = x)
#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(binding = x, std140)
#else
#define UNITY_LOCATION(x)
#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(std140)
#endif
uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(1) uniform UnityPerDraw {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_LODFade;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_WorldTransformParams;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_LightData;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_LightIndices[2];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_ProbesOcclusion;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_LightmapST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAr;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAg;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAb;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBr;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBg;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBb;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHC;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(0) uniform UnityPerMaterial {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _HairMap_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _BumpMapNr2_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RoughNessOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MetallicOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _NormalScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SHScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SHTopColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SHBotColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MainlightAttenuation;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _InvRim;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec3 _AddLightDir;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _AddlightColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _AddlightDarkcolor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AddlightScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AddlightAttenuation;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AddlightLerp;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RimlightScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RimlightScale2;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RimlightShadowScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _RimlightColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RimlightAttenuation;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _actorscale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cutoff;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _BumpScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Mask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _colorSkin;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AddlightShadowScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ActorScaleAttribute;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ShadowOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ShadowPow;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShiftOffuse1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShiftOffuse2;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShift;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_1Y;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _specularColor2;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MatColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MatMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SHColorScale;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump float u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat18;
float u_xlat19;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.xzw = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat0.xzw, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * vec3(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat1.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * u_xlat1.xxx;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_4 = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4 * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_5.z = u_xlat16_4 * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_5.xz);
    u_xlat16_4 = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4 = u_xlat16_4 * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4 = u_xlat16_4 * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4 = min(max(u_xlat16_4, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4 = clamp(u_xlat16_4, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4 * u_xlat16_4;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

#endif

#version 300 es

precision highp float;
precision highp int;
#define HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS 1
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
#define UNITY_UNIFORM
#else

#else
#define UNITY_LOCATION(x)
#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(std140)
#endif
uniform 	vec4 _MainLightPosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainLightColor;
uniform 	vec4 _Time;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[4];
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(0) uniform UnityPerMaterial {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _HairMap_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _BumpMapNr2_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RoughNessOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MetallicOffset;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _actorscale;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _BumpScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Mask;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AddlightShadowScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ActorScaleAttribute;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ShadowOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ShadowPow;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _EmisssionScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Emissive;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShiftOffuse1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShiftOffuse2;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShift;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _specularColor1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_1X;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_1Y;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _specularColor2;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_2X;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_2Y;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _shapeST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ShadowScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _RimLightDir;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _faceshadowScale;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _FresnelFactor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainPlayerPositionWS;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _RampMap_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _GhostChange;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MatColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MatMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SHColorScale;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _RampMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _GhostMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_7;
mediump float u_xlat16_21;
float u_xlat22;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat22);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat22) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.zxy) * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat22);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat22) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_0.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyw = u_xlat16_0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_0.xyw;
    u_xlat16_21 = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_21) * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat3.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat3.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = abs(u_xlat16_0.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_0.x = min(u_xlat16_0.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_7.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_7.x);
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xx * u_xlat3.xy;
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy + _Time.xx;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_GhostMap, u_xlat1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat16_0.x + (-_ShadowOffset);
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat22 * _ShadowPow;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat22 = min(max(u_xlat22, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat22 = clamp(u_xlat22, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_21 = (-u_xlat22) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_21 = u_xlat16_21 + u_xlat16_2.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_21 = min(max(u_xlat16_21, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_21 = clamp(u_xlat16_21, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat3.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_21) * vec2(_ShadowScale) + u_xlat16_7.xy;
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(_RampMap, u_xlat3.xy);
    u_xlat16_4 = u_xlat16_3 * _SHTopColor;
    u_xlat16_3 = u_xlat16_3 * _SHBotColor + (-u_xlat16_4);
    u_xlat16_3 = vec4(u_xlat16_21) * u_xlat16_3 + u_xlat16_4;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_21 * _SHBotColor.w + u_xlat16_3.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_7.x = min(max(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_7.x = clamp(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_7.x = dot(vec2(vec2(_Cutoff, _Cutoff)), u_xlat16_7.xx);
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat16_7.x + (-u_xlat16_0.x);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat22 = min(max(u_xlat22, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat22 = clamp(u_xlat22, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat22;
    u_xlat6.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_0.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = (-u_xlat16_3.xyz) + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(vec3(_Cutoff, _Cutoff, _Cutoff)) * u_xlat16_0.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(_GhostChange) * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    return;
}

#endif

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShiftOffuse1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShiftOffuse2;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShift;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _specularColor1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_1X;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_1Y;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _specularColor2;

#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec3 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
mediump float u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
float u_xlat21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_5 = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_5 * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.z = u_xlat16_5 * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xz);
    u_xlat16_5 = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_5 = u_xlat16_5 * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_5 = u_xlat16_5 * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_5 = min(max(u_xlat16_5, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_5 = clamp(u_xlat16_5, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_5 * u_xlat16_5;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

#endif

#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _HairMap_ST;

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _RampMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _GhostMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
bool u_xlatb7;
mediump float u_xlat16_9;
bool u_xlatb14;
vec2 u_xlat15;
mediump float u_xlat16_17;
float u_xlat21;
mediump float u_xlat16_23;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat0.xy,u_xlat0.z);
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat0, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_9 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_9;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_2.x + 0.75;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb7 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb7 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb14 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb14 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb7 = u_xlatb14 || u_xlatb7;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb7) ? 1.0 : u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_3.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_3.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_3.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat0.zxy) + (-u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat0.zxy) * u_xlat1.yzx;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat0.yzx) * u_xlat1.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_23 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_23 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_23);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_23) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.y = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot((-u_xlat0.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_23 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_23 = abs(u_xlat16_23) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_23 = min(u_xlat16_23, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xx * u_xlat4.xy;
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_23 + (-_ShadowOffset);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * _ShadowPow;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_17 = (-u_xlat0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_17 = u_xlat16_0.w + u_xlat16_17;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_17 = min(max(u_xlat16_17, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_17 = clamp(u_xlat16_17, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_17) * vec2(_ShadowScale) + u_xlat16_3.xy;
    u_xlat15.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy + _Time.xx;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = texture(_GhostMap, u_xlat15.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_RampMap, u_xlat1.xy);
    u_xlat16_5 = u_xlat16_1 * _SHTopColor;
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_1 * _SHBotColor + (-u_xlat16_5);
    u_xlat16_1 = vec4(u_xlat16_17) * u_xlat16_1 + u_xlat16_5;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_17 * _SHBotColor.w + u_xlat16_1.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_3.x = min(max(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_3.x = clamp(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(vec2(vec2(_Cutoff, _Cutoff)), u_xlat16_3.xx);
    u_xlat21 = (-u_xlat16_23) + u_xlat16_3.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat21 = min(max(u_xlat21, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat21 = clamp(u_xlat21, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat21;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xyz) + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(vec3(_Cutoff, _Cutoff, _Cutoff)) * u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-u_xlat16_2.xyz) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(_GhostChange) * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    return;
}

#endif

#ifdef VERTEX

uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;

varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
varying highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec3 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
mediump float u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
float u_xlat21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_5 = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_5 * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.z = u_xlat16_5 * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xz);
    u_xlat16_5 = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_5 = u_xlat16_5 * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_5 = u_xlat16_5 * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_5 = clamp(u_xlat16_5, 0.0, 1.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_5 * u_xlat16_5;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat0.xy).x;
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlat0.x<u_xlat0.z;
    u_xlat0.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat1.xy).x;
    u_xlatb1 = u_xlat1.x<u_xlat1.z;
    u_xlat0.y = (u_xlatb1) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat1.xy).x;
    u_xlatb1 = u_xlat1.x<u_xlat1.z;
    u_xlat0.z = (u_xlatb1) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat1.xy).x;
    u_xlatb1 = u_xlat1.x<u_xlat1.z;
    u_xlat0.w = (u_xlatb1) ? 0.0 : 1.0;

    u_xlat16_9 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_9;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_2.x + 0.75;
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlatb7 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
    u_xlatb14 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
    u_xlatb7 = u_xlatb14 || u_xlatb7;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb7) ? 1.0 : u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;

    u_xlat16_3.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_3.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);

    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat0.zxy) * u_xlat1.yzx;

    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_23 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_23 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_23);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_23) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.y = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot((-u_xlat0.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_23 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_23 = abs(u_xlat16_23) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_23 = min(u_xlat16_23, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xx * u_xlat4.xy;
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_23 + (-_ShadowOffset);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_17 = (-u_xlat0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_17 = u_xlat10_0.w + u_xlat16_17;
    u_xlat16_17 = clamp(u_xlat16_17, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat1.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_17) * vec2(_ShadowScale) + u_xlat16_3.xy;
    u_xlat15.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy + _Time.xx;
    u_xlat10_4.xyz = texture2D(_GhostMap, u_xlat15.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat10_1 = texture2D(_RampMap, u_xlat1.xy);
    u_xlat16_5 = u_xlat10_1 * _SHTopColor;
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat10_1 * _SHBotColor + (-u_xlat16_5);
    u_xlat16_1 = vec4(u_xlat16_17) * u_xlat16_1 + u_xlat16_5;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_17 * _SHBotColor.w + u_xlat16_1.w;
    u_xlat16_3.x = clamp(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(vec2(vec2(_Cutoff, _Cutoff)), u_xlat16_3.xx);
    u_xlat21 = (-u_xlat16_23) + u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat21 = clamp(u_xlat21, 0.0, 1.0);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat21;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat10_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xyz) + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(vec3(_Cutoff, _Cutoff, _Cutoff)) * u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-u_xlat16_2.xyz) + u_xlat10_4.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(_GhostChange) * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    return;
}

    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_5 = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_5 * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.z = u_xlat16_5 * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xz);
    u_xlat16_5 = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_5 = u_xlat16_5 * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_5 = u_xlat16_5 * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_5 = min(max(u_xlat16_5, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_5 = clamp(u_xlat16_5, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_5 * u_xlat16_5;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

#endif

    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat0.xy,u_xlat0.z);

    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);

#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlatb7 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);

#endif
    u_xlatb7 = u_xlatb14 || u_xlatb7;

    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;

    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat0.zxy) * u_xlat1.yzx;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat0.yzx) * u_xlat1.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);

    u_xlat4.y = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot((-u_xlat0.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_23 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_23 = abs(u_xlat16_23) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_23 = min(u_xlat16_23, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xx * u_xlat4.xy;
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_23 + (-_ShadowOffset);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * _ShadowPow;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_17 = (-u_xlat0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_17 = u_xlat16_0.w + u_xlat16_17;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_17 = min(max(u_xlat16_17, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_17 = clamp(u_xlat16_17, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_17) * vec2(_ShadowScale) + u_xlat16_3.xy;
    u_xlat15.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy + _Time.xx;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = texture(_GhostMap, u_xlat15.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_RampMap, u_xlat1.xy);
    u_xlat16_5 = u_xlat16_1 * _SHTopColor;
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_1 * _SHBotColor + (-u_xlat16_5);

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_3.x = min(max(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_3.x = clamp(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(vec2(vec2(_Cutoff, _Cutoff)), u_xlat16_3.xx);
    u_xlat21 = (-u_xlat16_23) + u_xlat16_3.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat21 = min(max(u_xlat21, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat21 = clamp(u_xlat21, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat21;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xyz) + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(vec3(_Cutoff, _Cutoff, _Cutoff)) * u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-u_xlat16_2.xyz) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(_GhostChange) * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    return;
}

uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainLightShadowParams;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _SHTopColor;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _SHBotColor;
uniform 	mediump float _Cutoff;
uniform 	mediump float _ShadowOffset;
uniform 	mediump float _ShadowPow;
uniform 	mediump float _ShadowScale;
uniform 	mediump float _GhostChange;
uniform lowp sampler2D _BumpMap;
uniform highp sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;
uniform lowp sampler2D _MainTex;
uniform lowp sampler2D _RampMap;
uniform lowp sampler2D _GhostMap;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
#define SV_Target0 gl_FragData[0]
vec4 u_xlat0;
lowp vec4 u_xlat10_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
lowp vec4 u_xlat10_1;
bool u_xlatb1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
lowp vec3 u_xlat10_4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_5;
lowp vec3 u_xlat10_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
bool u_xlatb7;
mediump float u_xlat16_9;
bool u_xlatb14;
vec2 u_xlat15;
mediump float u_xlat16_17;
float u_xlat21;
mediump float u_xlat16_23;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat0.xy).x;
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlat0.x<u_xlat0.z;
    u_xlat0.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat1.xy).x;
    u_xlatb1 = u_xlat1.x<u_xlat1.z;
    u_xlat0.y = (u_xlatb1) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat1.xy).x;
    u_xlatb1 = u_xlat1.x<u_xlat1.z;
    u_xlat0.z = (u_xlatb1) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat1.xy).x;
    u_xlatb1 = u_xlat1.x<u_xlat1.z;
    u_xlat0.w = (u_xlatb1) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat0, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_9 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_9;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_2.x + 0.75;
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlatb7 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
    u_xlatb14 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
    u_xlatb7 = u_xlatb14 || u_xlatb7;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb7) ? 1.0 : u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_3.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_3.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_3.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat0.zxy) + (-u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat0.zxy) * u_xlat1.yzx;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat0.yzx) * u_xlat1.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat10_5.xyz = texture2D(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_5.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_23 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_23 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_23);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_23) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.y = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot((-u_xlat0.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_23 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_23 = abs(u_xlat16_23) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_23 = min(u_xlat16_23, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xx * u_xlat4.xy;
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_23 + (-_ShadowOffset);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_17 = (-u_xlat0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_17 = u_xlat10_0.w + u_xlat16_17;
    u_xlat16_17 = clamp(u_xlat16_17, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat1.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_17) * vec2(_ShadowScale) + u_xlat16_3.xy;
    u_xlat15.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy + _Time.xx;
    u_xlat10_4.xyz = texture2D(_GhostMap, u_xlat15.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat10_1 = texture2D(_RampMap, u_xlat1.xy);
    u_xlat16_5 = u_xlat10_1 * _SHTopColor;
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat10_1 * _SHBotColor + (-u_xlat16_5);
    u_xlat16_1 = vec4(u_xlat16_17) * u_xlat16_1 + u_xlat16_5;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_17 * _SHBotColor.w + u_xlat16_1.w;
    u_xlat16_3.x = clamp(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(vec2(vec2(_Cutoff, _Cutoff)), u_xlat16_3.xx);
    u_xlat21 = (-u_xlat16_23) + u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat21 = clamp(u_xlat21, 0.0, 1.0);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat21;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat10_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xyz) + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(vec3(_Cutoff, _Cutoff, _Cutoff)) * u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-u_xlat16_2.xyz) + u_xlat10_4.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(_GhostChange) * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    return;
}

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec3 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
mediump float u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
float u_xlat21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_5 = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_5 * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.z = u_xlat16_5 * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xz);
    u_xlat16_5 = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_5 = u_xlat16_5 * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_5 = u_xlat16_5 * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_5 = min(max(u_xlat16_5, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_5 = clamp(u_xlat16_5, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_5 * u_xlat16_5;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;

mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat0.xy,u_xlat0.z);
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat0, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_9 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_9;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_2.x + 0.75;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb7 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb7 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb14 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb14 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb7 = u_xlatb14 || u_xlatb7;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb7) ? 1.0 : u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_3.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_3.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_3.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat0.zxy) + (-u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat0.zxy) * u_xlat1.yzx;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat0.yzx) * u_xlat1.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);

    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;

    u_xlat16_23 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_23);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_23) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.y = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot((-u_xlat0.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_23 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_23 = abs(u_xlat16_23) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_23 = min(u_xlat16_23, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xx * u_xlat4.xy;
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_23 + (-_ShadowOffset);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * _ShadowPow;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_17 = (-u_xlat0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_17 = u_xlat16_0.w + u_xlat16_17;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_17 = min(max(u_xlat16_17, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_17 = clamp(u_xlat16_17, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_17) * vec2(_ShadowScale) + u_xlat16_3.xy;
    u_xlat15.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy + _Time.xx;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = texture(_GhostMap, u_xlat15.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_RampMap, u_xlat1.xy);
    u_xlat16_5 = u_xlat16_1 * _SHTopColor;
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_1 * _SHBotColor + (-u_xlat16_5);
    u_xlat16_1 = vec4(u_xlat16_17) * u_xlat16_1 + u_xlat16_5;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_17 * _SHBotColor.w + u_xlat16_1.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_3.x = min(max(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_3.x = clamp(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(vec2(vec2(_Cutoff, _Cutoff)), u_xlat16_3.xx);
    u_xlat21 = (-u_xlat16_23) + u_xlat16_3.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat21 = min(max(u_xlat21, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat21 = clamp(u_xlat21, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat21;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xyz) + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(vec3(_Cutoff, _Cutoff, _Cutoff)) * u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-u_xlat16_2.xyz) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(_GhostChange) * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_23 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_23 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_23);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_23) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.y = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot((-u_xlat0.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_23 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_23 = abs(u_xlat16_23) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_23 = min(u_xlat16_23, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xx * u_xlat4.xy;
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_23 + (-_ShadowOffset);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_17 = (-u_xlat0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_17 = u_xlat10_0.w + u_xlat16_17;
    u_xlat16_17 = clamp(u_xlat16_17, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat1.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_17) * vec2(_ShadowScale) + u_xlat16_3.xy;
    u_xlat15.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy + _Time.xx;
    u_xlat10_4.xyz = texture2D(_GhostMap, u_xlat15.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat10_1 = texture2D(_RampMap, u_xlat1.xy);
    u_xlat16_5 = u_xlat10_1 * _SHTopColor;
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat10_1 * _SHBotColor + (-u_xlat16_5);
    u_xlat16_1 = vec4(u_xlat16_17) * u_xlat16_1 + u_xlat16_5;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_17 * _SHBotColor.w + u_xlat16_1.w;
    u_xlat16_3.x = clamp(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(vec2(vec2(_Cutoff, _Cutoff)), u_xlat16_3.xx);
    u_xlat21 = (-u_xlat16_23) + u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat21 = clamp(u_xlat21, 0.0, 1.0);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat21;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat10_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xyz) + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(vec3(_Cutoff, _Cutoff, _Cutoff)) * u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-u_xlat16_2.xyz) + u_xlat10_4.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(_GhostChange) * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    return;
}

#endif
"
